/////////////////////
// Suicide Bomber ///
// by Tormentor667 //
/////////////////////


actor SuicideBomber
{
	obituary "%o was killed by a crazy suicide bomber."
	health 40
	radius 20
	height 56
	mass 100
	speed 24
	painchance 20
	seesound "suicide/sit"
	attacksound "shotguy/death"
	painsound "shotguy/pain"
	deathsound "shotguy/death"
	MeleeRange 160
	MONSTER
	+FLOORCLIP
	states
	{
		Spawn:
			BMBE AB 10 A_Look
			loop
		See:
			BMBE AAABBBCCCDDD 2 A_Chase
			BMBE A 0 A_PlaySound("suicide/scream")
			loop
		Melee:
			BMBE A 0 A_PlaySound("KamikazeBeep", CHAN_AUTO)
			BMBE A 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE A 2 A_Recoil(-4)
			BMBE A 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE A 2 A_Recoil(-4)
			BMBE B 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE B 2 A_Recoil(-4)
			BMBE B 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE B 2 A_Recoil(-4)
			BMBE C 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE C 2 A_Recoil(-3)
			BMBE C 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE C 2 A_Recoil(-3)
			BMBE D 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE D 2 A_Recoil(-3)
			BMBE D 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE D 2 A_Recoil(-3)
			BMBE A 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE A 2 A_Recoil(-3)
			BMBE A 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE A 2 A_Recoil(-3)
			BMBE B 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE B 2 A_Recoil(-3)
			BMBE B 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE B 2 A_Recoil(-3)
			BMBE C 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE C 2 A_Recoil(-3)
			BMBE C 0 A_FaceTarget
			BMBE C 2 A_Recoil(-3)
			BMBE A 0 A_Die
			goto Death
		Pain:
			BMBE A 3
			BMBE A 3 A_Pain
			goto See
		Death:
			BMBE M 5 bright A_PlaySound("KamikazeBoom", CHAN_AUTO)
			TNT1 A 0 A_Explode (75, 160)
			TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile ("XDeath1", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile ("XDeath2", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile ("XDeath3", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile ("XDeath4", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 AAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile ("SuperWallRedBlood", 40, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (-5, 5))
			TNT1 AAAA 0 A_CustomMissile ("Instestin", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile ("Brutal_FlyingBlood", 35, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 AAAAAA 0 bright A_CustomMissile ("SuperGoreSpawner", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (50, 130))
			BMBE N 5 bright A_XScream
			TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile ("GiantBloodSpot", 4, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			BMBE O 5 A_NoBlocking
			BMBE PQRST 5
			BMBE U -1
			stop
		Ice:
			BMBE A 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
			BMBE A 1 A_FreezeDeathchunks
			wait
		Rise:
			TFOG ABABCD 4 BRIGHT
			Goto See	
	}
}

//Flamer zombie + Projectiles
ACTOR FlamerZombie
{
    Health 30
    Radius 20
    Height 56
    Speed 8
    PainChance 100

    {

        FLMZ E 10 A_FaceTarget
      	FLMZ FFF 1 A_CustomMissile("ZombieFire",32,0,random(-4,4),0)

      	FLMZ FFF 1 A_CustomMissile("ZombieFire",32,0,random(-4,4),0)
        FLMZ E 10 A_FaceTarget
      	FLMZ FFF 1 A_CustomMissile("ZombieFire",32,0,random(-4,4),0)

        FLMZ J 5 A_Fall
        FLMZ K 5

    FLMZ G 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
	FLMZ G 1 A_FreezeDeathchunks
    wait
    Raise:
        FLMZ KJIH 5
        Goto See
    }
}

ACTOR ZombieFire
{
   Radius 2
   Height 4
   Speed 16
   Damage (2)
   PROJECTILE
   RENDERSTYLE ADD
   DamageType Fire
   ALPHA 0.67
   Scale 0.67
   SeeSound "weapons/flamer"
   DeathSound "weapons/scorch"
   +THRUGHOST
   States
   {
   Spawn:
      NULL A 2 Bright
      FRFX AAABBBCCCDDD 2 Bright A_Explode(1,8,0)
      FRFX D 0 Bright A_Lowgravity
      FRFX EEEFFFGGG 2 Bright A_Explode(1,16,0)
      FRFX HHHIIIJJJ 2 Bright A_Explode(1,32,0)
      FRFX KKKLLLMMM 2 Bright A_Explode(1,64,0)
      FRFX NNNOOO 2 Bright
      stop
   Death:
      FRFX HIJ 2 Bright A_Explode(1,32,0)
      FRFX J 0 A_CustomMissile ("ZombieDropFire",0,0,0,4)
      FRFX KLM 2 Bright A_Explode(1,64,0)
      FRFX NO 2 Bright
      stop
   }
}

ACTOR ZombieDropFire
{
   Radius 8
   Height 40
   PROJECTILE
   RENDERSTYLE ADD
   DamageType Fire
   ALPHA 0.90
   -NOGRAVITY
   +LOWGRAVITY
   +NOEXPLODEFLOOR
   +NODAMAGETHRUST
   +THRUGHOST
   States
   {
   Spawn:
      FLME A 1 Bright A_Playsound("weapons/onfire")
      FLME A 1 Bright A_Explode(5,16,0)
      FLME BCDEFGHIJKLMN 2 Bright A_Explode(5,16,0)
      FLME A 1 Bright A_Playsound("weapons/onfire")
      FLME A 1 Bright A_Explode(5,32,0)
      FLME BCDEFGHIJKLMN 2 Bright A_Explode(5,16,0)
      FLME A 1 Bright A_Playsound("weapons/onfire")
      FLME A 1 Bright A_Explode(5,32,0)
      FLME BCDEFGHIJKLMN 2 Bright A_Explode(5,16,0)
      FLME A 1 Bright A_Playsound("weapons/onfire")
      FLME A 1 Bright A_Explode(5,32,0)
      FLME BCDEFGHIJKLMN 2 Bright A_Explode(5,16,0)
      FLME A 1 Bright A_Playsound("weapons/onfire")
      FLME A 1 Bright A_Explode(5,32,0)
      FLME BCDEFGHIJKLMN 2 Bright A_Explode(5,16,0)
      FLME A 0 A_Jump(192,1)
      loop
      NULL A 0
      goto death
   Death:
      NULL A 1 Bright
      stop
   }
}

//BFG zombieman

actor BFGGuy
{
	obituary "%o was vapourized by a zombie's BFG9000."
	health 30
	radius 20
	height 56
	mass 100
	speed 8
	painchance 170
	seesound "chainguy/sight"
	painsound "chainguy/pain"
	deathsound "chainguy/death"
	activesound "chainguy/active"
	Dropitem "Clip"
	Dropitem "Shotgun"
	Dropitem "Chaingun"
	Dropitem "Cell"
	Dropitem "bfg9000" 20
	MONSTER
	+FLOORCLIP
	states
	{
		Spawn:
			BFGZ AB 10 A_Look
			loop
		See:
			BFGZ AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
			loop
		Missile:
			BFGZ E 0 A_FaceTarget
			BFGZ E 35 A_PlaySound ("9kbfg")
			BFGZ F 10 Bright
			BFGZ F 10 Bright A_CustomMissile("MonsterBFG", 32, 0, 0)
			BFGZ E 20
			goto See
		Pain:
			BFGZ G 3
			BFGZ G 3 A_Pain
			goto See
		Death:
			BFGZ H 5
			BFGZ I 5 A_Scream
			BFGZ J 5 A_NoBlocking
			BFGZ KLM 5
			BFGZ N -1
			stop
		XDeath:
			BFGZ O 5
			TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile ("XDeath1", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile ("XDeath2", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 AA 0 A_CustomMissile ("XDeath3", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile ("XDeath4", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 AAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile ("SuperWallRedBlood", 40, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (-5, 5))
			TNT1 AAAA 0 A_CustomMissile ("Instestin", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile ("Brutal_FlyingBlood", 35, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (0, 160))
			TNT1 AAAAAA 0 bright A_CustomMissile ("SuperGoreSpawner", 32, 0, random (0, 360), 2, random (50, 130))
			BFGZ P 5 A_XScream
			BFGZ Q 5 A_NoBlocking
			BFGZ RS 5
			BFGZ T -1
			stop
		Ice:
			BFGZ G 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
			BFGZ G 1 A_FreezeDeathchunks
			wait
		Raise:
			BFGZ NMLKJIH 5
			goto See
	}
}

ACTOR RailArachnotron
{
	//$Category "ZDoom Monster pack"
	Health 500
	Radius 64
	Height 64
	Mass 600
	Speed 12
	PainChance 192
	Damage 30
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	+Bossdeath
	+NEVERFAST
	Dropitem "RailgunGiver" 128
	SeeSound "baby/sight"
	PainSound "baby/pain"
	DeathSound "baby/death"
	ActiveSound "baby/active"
	Obituary "%o was railed by an arachnotron."
	Decal RedRailScorch
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		RSPI AB 10 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		RSPI A 20
		RSPI A 3 A_BabyMetal
		RSPI ABBCC 3 A_Chase
		RSPI D 3 A_BabyMetal
		RSPI DEEFF 3 A_Chase
		Goto See+1
	Missile:
		RSPI A 0 A_PlaySound ("baby/chargerailgun")
		RSPI AAAA 4 A_FaceTarget(0, 0)
		RSPI GGGG 4 A_FaceTarget(0, 0)
		RSPI G 4
		RSPI H 4 A_CustomRailgun (30, 0, BB0000, FF0000, RGF_FULLBRIGHT, 0)
		RSPI G 8
		Goto See+1
	Pain:
		RSPI I 3
		RSPI I 3 A_Pain
		Goto See+1
	Death:
		RSPI J 20 A_Scream
		RSPI K 7 A_Fall
		RSPI LMNO 7
		RSPI P -1 A_bossdeath
		Stop
	Ice:
		RSPI I 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
		RSPI I 1 A_FreezeDeathchunks
		wait
	Raise:
		RSPI P 5
		RSPI ONMLKJ 5
		Goto See+1
	}
}

//SSG Zombieman

ACTOR SSGZombie
{

actor AracnorbQueen
{
	//$Category Monsters
	//$Title "Aracnorb Queen"
	Species "Brain"
	MONSTER
	+NOGRAVITY
	+FLOAT
	+FLOATBOB
	+BOSS
	+Dontrip
	Health 2500
	Radius 34
	Height 76
	Mass 2000
	Speed 12
	PainChance 45
	SeeSound "queen/sight"
	ActiveSound "queen/active"
	PainSound "queen/pain"
	DeathSound "queen/death"
	MeleeSound "queen/melee"
	Dropitem "bfg9000" 50
	MeleeDamage 6
	MissileHeight 36
	Obituary "%o suffered psychic trauma from an aracnorb queen's brainwaves."
	HitObituary "%o had %p skull chewed by an aracnorb queen."
	Scale 0.85
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			ARNQ A 1 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			ARNQ A 2 A_Chase
			Loop
		Melee:
			ARNQ ABC 5
			ARNQ D 6 A_MeleeAttack
			Goto See
		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(96, "BFG")
			TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(512, "CloseRange")
			Goto LongRange
		CloseRange:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(176, "RapidFire")
			Goto SpreadFire
		LongRange:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(176, "SpreadFire")
			Goto RapidFire
		BFG:
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("queen/fire")
			ARNQ BCD 8 A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 10 Bright A_CustomMissile("QueenBFG",50,-10,0)
			Goto See
		RapidFire:
			ARNQ BCD 8 A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 5 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-4,4))
			ARNQ D 0 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 5 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-4,4))
			ARNQ D 0 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 5 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-4,4))
			ARNQ D 0 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 5 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-4,4))
			ARNQ P 0 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 5 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-4,4))
			ARNQ D 0 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 5 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-4,4))
			ARNQ D 0 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 5 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-4,4))
			ARNQ D 0 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 5 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-4,4))
			ARNQ D 0 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 5 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-4,4))
			ARNQ D 0 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 5 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-4,4))
			ARNQ D 0 BRIGHT A_FaceTarget
			ARNQ E 5 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile ("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-4,4))
			ARNQ D 5 A_FaceTarget
			//ARNQ D 5
			Goto See
		SpreadFire:
			ARNQ BCD 8 A_FaceTarget
			TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("QueenPlasmaBlast", 40, 0, random(-7,7), CMF_AIMOFFSET|CMF_OFFSETPITCH, random(-3,3))

  Monster
  +NoGravity
  +NoBlood
  +Float
  +DontHurtSpecies
  Obituary "%o was scorched by an Afrit"
  HitObituary "%o found the Afrit too hot to handle."
  Damagefactor "HellFire", 0.0
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    FRIT A 0
    FRIT A 0 A_CustomMissile("OrbitComet", 44, 0, 0, 2, 0)
    FRIT A 0 A_CustomMissile("OrbitComet2", 44, 0, 180, 2, 0)
    FRIT AABB 4 Bright A_Look
    Goto Spawn+3
  Idle:
    FRIT ABCD 4 Bright A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    FRIT AABBCCDD 2 Bright A_Chase
    Loop
  Melee:
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jumpifcloser(128, "Melee2")
    FRIT ST 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
    FRIT U 6 Bright A_CustomComboAttack("RedBaronball", 44, 10, "Baron/Melee")
    Goto See
  Melee2:
    FRIT E 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
    FRIT F 6 Bright A_CustomMissile("HellFire", 44)
    FRIT G 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
    Goto See
  Missile:
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64, "Missile3")
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128, "Missile2")
    FRIT ST 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
    FRIT U 6 Bright A_CustomComboAttack("RedBaronBall", 44, 10, "Baron/Melee")
    Goto See
  Missile2:
    FRIT EF 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
    FRIT G 6 Bright A_CustomMissile("Comet", 44)
    Goto See
  Missile3:
    TNT1 A 0 A_Jumpifcloser(128, "Melee2")
    FRIT E 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
	FRIT G 0 A_CustomMissile ("BaronBall_Fire", 48, 0, random(-7, 7))
	FRIT G 0 A_CustomMissile ("BaronBall_Fire", 48, 0, random(-7, 7))
	FRIT G 0 A_CustomMissile ("BaronBall_Fire", 48, 0, random(-7, 7))
    FRIT G 6 Bright A_FaceTarget
    Goto See
  Pain:
    FRIT H 4 Bright
    FRIT H 4 Bright A_Pain
    Goto See
  Death:
    TNT1 A 0 A_NoGravity
    FRIT I 6 Bright A_Scream
    FRIT J 5 Bright A_NoBlocking
    FRIT KLMNOPQR 4 Bright
    Stop
  }
}

    SIMP J 8 A_Scream

    SIMP L 6 A_NoBlocking
    SIMP M 140
	SIMP M -1 A_SpawnItem ("HealImp")
    stop
	Ice:
    SIMP H 5 A_GenericFreezeDeath
    SIMP H 1 A_FreezeDeathchunks
    wait
  Death:
    SIMP A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Shell",1,2)
	Goto DeathRaise

	SIMP A 0 A_SpawnItem("ImpGhostOut")

    SIMP K 6
    SIMP L 6 A_NoBlocking
    SIMP M -1
    stop

    stop

actor SpImpBall
{
  Radius 6
  Height 8
  Projectile
  +RANDOMIZE
  RenderStyle Add
  Alpha 1
  SeeSound "timeball/attack"
  DeathSound "timeball/hit"
  Speed 25
  damage 5
  +NOTIMEFREEZE
  states
  {
  Spawn:
    SBLA A 1 A_SpawnItem("SpBallTrailA",-12)
    SBLA A 2 bright
	SBLA B 1 A_SpawnItem("SpBallTrailB",-12)
	SBLA B 2 bright
    loop
  Death:
    SBLA CDE 6 bright
    stop
  }
}

//The Inferno Demon is a mighty demon with full control over the power of fire. This monster took a shit load of time to create and perfect, I hope you like it.
//I recommend to use it only as a boss like monster as it is extremely powerful and can kill you really fast if you haven't mastered dodging. He can't hurt himself
//cause he uses a damage type and is resistant to his own damage type. He has about 5 attacks, one of which has about 20 different combinations.

ACTOR InfernoDemon
{
	Health 8000
	Speed 16
	Radius 40
	Height 115
	Mass 5000
	Damage 15
	BloodColor "Orange"
	Monster
	PainChance 4
	damagefactor "Inferno", 0
	SeeSound "Infdem/see"
	PainSound "Infdem/pain"
	DeathSound "Infdem/death"
	ActiveSound "Infdem/active"
	Attacksound "Infdem/Attack"
	DropItem "Gastersummon"
	Obituary "%o was sent to burn in the fires of hell for an eternity."
	
	+MISSILEMORE
	+MISSILEEVENMORE
	+BOSS
	+FLOORCLIP
	+TELESTOMP
	+DONTMORPH
	+NOTARGET
	+NOICEDEATH
	+FIXMAPTHINGPOS
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		DIAB A 5 A_Look
		Loop
	See:
		DIAB A 0 A_PlaySound("KoraxStep")
		DIAB A 0 Radius_Quake(10,5,0,10,0)
		DIAB AB 6 A_Chase
		DIAB C 0 A_PlaySound("KoraxStep")
		DIAB C 0 Radius_Quake(10,5,0,10,0)
		DIAB CD 6 A_Chase
		Goto See
	Missile:
		DIAB A 1 A_Playsound("Infdem/Attack")
		DIAB A 2 Bright A_FaceTarget
		DIAB A 0 A_Jump(256, "FirePuff", "MeteorBolt", "InfernoBomb", "FireBeam", "FireGlyph", "LavaBall", "LavaBall2", "LavaBall3", "LavaBall4", "LavaBall5", "LavaBall6", "LavaBall7", "DemonMeteor", "DemonMeteor2", "DemonMeteor3", "DemonMeteor4", "DemonMeteor5", "DemonMeteor6", "DemonMeteor7", "AllShit", "WomboCombo", "WomboCombo2", "WomboCombo3", "WomboCombo4", "WomboCombo5", "WomboCombo6")
		DIAB A -1
		goto See
		
	FirePuff:
		DIAB G 2 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("FirePuff",-24,0,96,0,0,5,128)
		DIAB G 2 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("FirePuff",-24,0,96,0,0,5,128)
		DIAB G 2 Bright A_SpawnItemEx("FirePuff",-24,0,96,0,0,5,128)

ACTOR PyroZombie
{
	obituary "%o was flambeed by a Pyro Zombie."
	health 100
	radius 20
	height 56
	mass 100
	speed 8
	painchance 170
	ReactionTime 10
	seesound "chainguy/sight"
	painsound "chainguy/pain"
	deathsound "chainguy/death"
	activesound "chainguy/active"
	missiletype PyroShot
	MONSTER
	Dropitem "Nukecharge"
	+FLOORCLIP
	states
	{
		Spawn:
			PYRZ AB 10 A_Look
			loop
		See:
			PYRZ AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
			loop
		Missile:
			PYRZ E 1 Bright A_PlaySound("weapons/nuclearmissilecharge", CHAN_AUTO, 1.0, false, 0.5)
			PYRZ E 10 A_FaceTarget
			PYRZ F 10 Bright
			PYRZ F 0 Bright A_PlaySound("PyroCannon/Fire", CHAN_AUTO, 1.0, false, 0.5)
			PYRZ F 10 Bright A_PlaySound("weapons/nuclearmissilefire", CHAN_WEAPON, 1.0, false, 0.5)
			PYRZ E 10 Bright A_MissileAttack
			goto See
		Pain:
			PYRZ G 3
			PYRZ G 3 A_Pain
			goto See
		Death:
			PYRZ H 5
			PYRZ I 5 A_Scream
			PYRZ J 5 A_NoBlocking
			PYRZ KLM 5
			PYRZ N -1
			stop
		XDeath:
			PYRZ O 5
			PYRZ P 5 A_XScream
			PYRZ Q 5 A_NoBlocking
			PYRZ RS 5
			PYRZ T -1
			stop
		Raise:
			PYRZ NMLKJIH 5
			goto See
	}
}

actor DivineShadow : SH_BaseMonster
{
	//$Category Monsters
	//$Sprite VIL2G1
	//$Title Divine Shadow

	Health 600
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Mass 500
	Speed 20
	PainChance 0
	BloodColor "00 80 00"

	DamageFactor BFGSplash, 0.5

	Species "DivineShadow"

	//RenderStyle Add
	//Alpha 0.5

	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+FLOORCLIP
	+NOTARGET

	SeeSound "vile/sight"
	PainSound "vile/pain"
	DeathSound "vile/death"
	ActiveSound "vile/active"
	MeleeSound "vile/stop"

	Obituary "%o was disintegrated by a Divine Shadow."

	States
	{
	Spawn:
		VIL1 A 0 NoDelay A_SetUserVar("user_extralife_chance", 75)
		goto SpawnLoop
	SpawnLoop:
		VIL1 AB 10 A_Look
		loop
	See:
		VIL1 AABBCC 2 A_Chase
		loop

	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(64, "MissileLoopStart")
		//goto MissileSingle

	MissileSingle:
		TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("DivineShadow::HoldVile", 0, 0, 0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_CustomMissile("DivineShadowAtkLarge", 50.0, 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/bfgf")
		VIL2 G 4 BRIGHT
		VIL2 HIJKLMNONP 4 BRIGHT
		goto See

	MissileLoopStart:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("DivineShadow::Circle", 0, 0, 0, 0)
		goto MissileLoop

	MissileLoop:
		VIL2 A 1 BRIGHT
		loop

	Death:
		VIL3 R 7 A_Scream
		VIL3 S 7 A_NoBlocking
		VIL3 TUWVXY 7
		VIL3 Z -1
		stop
	}
}

ACTOR Poe
{
	Health 500
	Radius 31
	Height 56
	Mass 800
	Speed 8
	PainChance 32
	Monster
	+FLOAT +NOGRAVITY +THRUGHOST +GHOST +NOICEDEATH +CANTSEEK
	bloodcolor "ff 0f 83"
	SeeSound "Poe/sight"
	PainSound "Poe/pain"
	DeathSound "Poe/death"
	ActiveSound "Poe/active"
	MeleeSound "imp/melee"
	MeleeDamage 4
	Obituary "%o is shocked to find out that ghosts are real"//who you gonna call? GHOSTBUSTERS!!!
	HitObituary "%o's soul was consumed by the Poe"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory ("PoeSpawnCookie", 1, "Look")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory ("PoeSpawnCookie")
		TNT1 A 0 A_changeflag (INVULNERABLE,1)
		TNT1 A 1 A_SetTranslucent (0,0)
		goto look
        Look:
        	POE1 A 0 A_KillChildren
        	POE1 A 3 A_look
        	loop
	See:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory ("PoeSpawnCookie2", 1, "See2")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory ("PoeSpawnCookie2")
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.1,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.2,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.3,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.4,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.5,0)
		POE1 A 0 A_changeflag (INVULNERABLE,0)
		goto See2
	See2:
		POE1 AAAAA 3 A_Chase
		POE1 A 0 A_JUMP (40, "SpawnClones")
		POE1 AA 3 A_Chase
		loop
	See3:
		POE1 AAA 3 A_Chase
		loop
	SpawnClones:
		POE1 A 0 A_KillChildren
		POE1 A 0 A_changeflag (INVULNERABLE,1)
		POE1 A 0 A_changeflag (FRIGHTENED,1)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.4,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.3,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.2,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.1,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0,0)
		POE1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Wander
		POE1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx ("FakePoe1",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,48)
		POE1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Wander
		POE1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx ("FakePoe2",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,48)
		POE1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Wander
		POE1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx ("FakePoe3",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,48)
		POE1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Wander
		POE1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx ("FakePoe4",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,48)
		POE1 AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_Wander
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.1,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.2,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.3,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.4,0)
		POE1 A 3 A_SetTranslucent (0.5,0)
		POE1 A 0 A_changeflag (INVULNERABLE,0)
		POE1 A 0 A_Changeflag (FRIGHTENED,0)
		goto See3
	Missile:
		POE1 E 0 A_JUMP (65, "Missile3")
		POE1 E 0 A_JUMP (125, "Missile2")
                POE1 EF 5 A_FaceTarget
                POE1 G 5 bright A_CustomMissile("PoeBall",24,0,0,0,0)
		Goto See2
	Missile2:
                POE1 EF 5 A_FaceTarget
                POE1 G 5 bright A_CustomMissile("PoeBall",24,0,0,0,0)
                POE1 G 0 bright A_CustomMissile("PoeBall",24,0,15,0,0)
                POE1 G 0 bright A_CustomMissile("PoeBall",24,0,-15,0,0)
		Goto See2
	Missile3:
                POE1 EF 5 A_FaceTarget
                POE1 G 5 bright A_CustomMissile("PoeTracer",24,0,0,0,0)
		Goto See2
	Melee:
		POE1 AEF 5 A_FaceTarget
		POE1 G 5 A_MeleeAttack
		goto See2
	Pain:
		POE1 H 3
		POE1 H 3 A_Pain
		POE1 I 0 A_KillChildren
		POE1 I 6
		Goto See2
	Death:
		POE1 J 0 A_changeflag (NOGRAVITY,1)
		POE1 K 8
		POE1 L 8 A_Scream
		POE1 M 0 A_KillChildren
		POE1 N 8 A_SetTranslucent (0.4,0)
		POE1 O 8 A_SetTranslucent (0.3,0)
		POE1 P 8 A_SetTranslucent (0.2,0)
		POE1 Q 8 A_SetTranslucent (0.1,0)
		POE1 R 8 A_SetTranslucent (0,0)
		TNT1 S 8 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 L -1 A_SetFloorClip
		Stop
	}
}

actor Rictus
{
  obituary "%o was charred by a rictus."
  health 100
  radius 16
  height 56
  mass 50
  speed 2
  missiletype RictusBall
  missileheight 0
  painchance 128
  seesound "rictus/sight"
  deathsound "rictus/death"
  activesound "rictus/active"
  painsound "rictus/pain"
  MONSTER
  +FLOAT
  +NOGRAVITY
  +NOICEDEATH
  +NOBLOOD
  +DONTFALL
  +FIRERESIST
  +DONTHURTSPECIES
  states
  {
  Spawn:
    RICT A 1 A_Look
    RICT AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT A 0 A_LoopActiveSound
    loop
  See:
    RICT A 1 A_Chase
    RICT AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT A 0 A_LoopActiveSound
    loop
  Missile:
    RICT A 0 A_LoopActiveSound
    RICT A 0 A_JumpIfHealthLower (25,25)
    RICT A 1 A_FaceTarget
    RICT AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT A 1 A_FaceTarget
    RICT AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT A 1 A_FaceTarget
    RICT AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT A 1 A_FaceTarget
    RICT AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT B 1 A_MissileAttack
    RICT BB 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT B 1
    RICT BB 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT B 1
    RICT BB 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT B 1
    RICT BB 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    goto See
    RICT A 0 A_CustomMissile (RictusKamakazi,0,0,0,0,0)
    RICT A 1 A_Die("Kamikaze")
    goto Death+7
  Pain:
    RICT B 1
    RICT BB 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT B 1
    RICT BB 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT B 1
    RICT BB 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT B 1 A_Pain
    RICT BB 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT B 1
    RICT BB 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    RICT B 1
    RICT BB 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 2, 0, random(1,-1) , random(90,270), 160, 0)
    goto See
  Death:
    TNT1 A 1 A_ScreamAndUnblock
    TNT1 AAAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx (RictusFire, random(1,-1), random(1,-1), random(1,-1), 6, 0, random(1,-1) , random(0,360), 128, 0)
    stop
  Death.Kamikaze:
    TNT1 A 1
    TNT1 A 1 A_NoBlocking
    stop
  }
}

ACTOR DarkInquisitor : Inquisitor
{
    SeeSound "darkinquisitor/sight"
    ActiveSound "darkinquisitor/active"
    DeathSound "darkinquisitor/death"
	PainSound "darkinquisitor/pain"
    Health 3000 //If using in Strife, reduce to 1200.
	Obituary "%o was executed by a Dark Inquisitor."
    PainChance 1
    Speed 20
    FloatSpeed 15
    Damagefactor "EMP", 0
    Damagefactor "Disintegrate", 0
	var int user_inflight; // Used to keep the Dark Inquisitor in the air even when in pain or attacking.
	+BOSS
    +BOSSDEATH
    +FLOORCLIP
    +NORADIUSDMG
    +DONTMORPH
    +NOICEDEATH
    +MISSILEMORE
    +MISSILEEVENMORE
    +DROPOFF
    States
    {
    Spawn:
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("Float", 0)
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NoGravity", 0)
		ROB4 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_inflight", 0)
		ROB4 A 10 A_Look
		Loop
    See:
		ROB4 B 6 A_Chase
		ROB4 C 0 A_playsoundEX("darkinquisitor/step","SoundSlot6")
		ROB4 C 6 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(z - floorz > 45, "Fly")//Lets it fly if it falls off a high enough ledge.
		ROB4 A 0 A_Jump(5,"TakeOff")
		ROB4 D 6 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(z - floorz > 45, "Fly")
		ROB4 A 0 A_Jump(5,"TakeOff")
		ROB4 E 6 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(z - floorz > 45, "Fly")
		ROB4 A 0 A_Jump(5,"TakeOff")
		ROB4 D 0 A_playsoundEX("darkinquisitor/step","SoundSlot6")
		ROB4 D 6 A_chase
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(z - floorz > 45, "Fly")
		ROB4 A 0 A_Jump(5,"TakeOff")
		ROB4 C 6 A_Chase
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(z - floorz > 45, "Fly")
		ROB4 A 0 A_Jump(5,"TakeOff")
		Goto See
	TakeOff: //Thanks for the code, Ghastly! ^^
		ROB4 A 8
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NoPain", 1)
		ROB4 I 8 ThrustThingZ(0, 42, 0, 1)
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(Float, 1)
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(NoGravity, 1)
		ROB4 H 8
		ROB4 A 0 A_Stop
		ROB4 A 0 A_PlaySound("darkinquisitor/flight")
		ROB4 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_inflight", 1)
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NoPain", 0)
		Goto Fly
	Land:
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NoPain", 1)
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("Float", 0)
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NoGravity", 0)
		ROB4 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_inflight", 0)
		ROB4 A 3 A_CheckFloor(1)
		Goto Land+4
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NoPain", 0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_StopSoundEx("SoundSlot6")
		Goto See
	Fly:
		ROB4 H 1 Bright A_PlaySoundEx("darkinquisitor/flight","SoundSlot6",1,0)
		ROB4 H 3 Bright A_Chase ("", "Missile", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_JumpIf(z - floorz < 45, "Land")	//If low enough, it lands safely on the ground.
		ROB4 A 0 A_Jump(1,"Land")
		ROB4 I 4 Bright A_Chase ("", "Missile")
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_JumpIf(z - floorz < 45, "Land")
		ROB4 A 0 A_Jump(1,"Land")
		ROB4 H 4 Bright A_Chase ("", "Missile", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_JumpIf(z - floorz < 45, "Land")
		ROB4 A 0 A_Jump(1,"Land")
		ROB4 I 4 Bright A_Chase ("", "Missile")
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_JumpIf(z - floorz < 45, "Land")
		ROB4 A 0 A_Jump(1,"Land")
		ROB4 H 4 Bright A_Chase ("", "Missile", 1)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright A_JumpIf(z - floorz < 45, "Land")
		ROB4 A 0 A_Jump(1,"Land")
		Loop
    Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(80,2)
		ROB4 A 0 A_JumpIfCloser(850,"EMP")
		ROB4 A 6 A_FaceTarget
		ROB4 F 0 Bright A_PlaySound("darkinquisitor/darkmatterfire")
		ROB4 F 4 Bright A_CustomMissile("DarkMatterBall",64,-32,0)
		ROB4 G 6
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_inflight == 1, "Fly")
		Goto See
	EMP:
		ROB4 A 6 A_FaceTarget
		ROB4 J 0 Bright A_PlaySound("darkinquisitor/empfire")
		ROB4 J 0 Bright A_CustomMissile("EMPGrenade",100,24,0,1)
		ROB4 J 3 Bright A_CustomMissile("EMPGrenade",100,-24,0,1)
		ROB4 G 6
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_inflight == 1, "Fly")
		Goto See
    Pain:
        ROB4 G 6
        ROB4 G 6 A_Pain
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIf(user_inflight == 1, "Fly")
        Goto See
    Death:
		ROB4 A 0 A_SetUserVar("user_inflight", 0)
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag ("FLOAT", 0)
		ROB4 A 0 A_ChangeFlag ("NOGRAVITY", 0)
		ROB4 A 0 A_StopSoundEx("SoundSlot6")
		ROB4 L 1 A_NoBlocking
		ROB4 LLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLLL 5 Bright A_CustomMissile("InquisitorDeathExplosion",0+random(20,120),0,0+random(0,370),0)
		ROB4 L 1 A_Scream
		NULL AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_CustomMissile("DarkInquisitorGibber",50,0,random(0,359))
		NULL A 0 A_CustomMissile("DarkInquisitorBigExplosion",0,0,0)
		TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(8,40,0,35,0)
        Stop
    }
}

actor Shrapnel1
{
    +DOOMBOUNCE
    PROJECTILE
    -NOGRAVITY
    +NOBLOCKMAP
    +CANNOTPUSH
    -NOTELEPORT
    -SOLID
	+GRENADETRAIL
    Radius 2
    Damage 4
    mass 5
    bouncefactor 0.5
    SeeSound "darkinquisitor/shrapnel"
    Speed 25
    States
    {
    Spawn:
        SHRP L 0
        SHRP L 0 A_Jump(64,"Alt")
        SHRP L 0 ThrustThingZ (0, (Random (20, 100)), 0, 1)
        goto See
    Alt:
    	SHRP M 0 ThrustThingZ (0, (Random (40, 130)), 0, 1)
    	Stop
    See:
        SHRP L 5
        SHRP L 5 ThrustThingZ(0,(Random (6, 20)),1,1)
        SHRP L 5
        SHRP L 5
        loop
    Death:
        SHRP L 0
        SHRP L 0
        SHRP L 0
        SHRP L 70
        Stop
    }
}

			Goto Missile+7

			Goto See

			FRGO E 3 Bright
			FRGO E 3 Bright A_Pain
			Goto See
		Death:
			FRGO E 0 A_ChangeFlag("FloatBob", 0)
			FRGO E 0 A_Stop
			FRGO EF 4 Bright

			FRGO H 6 Bright

	}

		FFAG I 3 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("FFslimeball6", 34, -32, random(-3,3), CMF_OFFSETPITCH, random(2,5))
		FFAG I 0 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("FFslimeball7", 34, 32, random(-3,3), CMF_OFFSETPITCH, random(1,5))
		FFAG I 3 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("FFslimeball8", 34, -32, random(-3,3), CMF_OFFSETPITCH, random(1,4))
		FFAG FG 6 A_FaceTarget
		Goto See
	Pain:
		FFAG J 3
		FFAG J 3 A_Pain
		Goto See
	Death:
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(FLOATBOB, 0)
		FFAG K 6 A_SetFloorClip
		FFAG L 6 A_Scream
		FFAG M 6 A_NoBlocking
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("flyingfatso/jetoff")
		FFAG NOPQRS 6
		FFAG T -1 A_BossDeath
	    Stop
	Raise:
	 	TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("flyingfatso/jeton")
		FFAG R 5 A_UnSetFloorClip
		FFAG QPONMLK 5
		TNT1 A 0 A_ChangeFlag(FLOATBOB, 1)
		Goto See
	}
}

    }

ACTOR ChainmailEttin
{
  Game Hexen
  Health 500
  Radius 25
  Height 68
  Mass 175
  Speed 15
  +Alwaysfast
  PainChance 60
  Monster
  +FLOORCLIP
  +TELESTOMP
  MeleeThreshold 196
  SeeSound "EttinSight"
  AttackSound "EttinSwing"
  PainSound "EttinPain"
  DeathSound "EttinDeath"
  ActiveSound "EttinActive"
  HowlSound "PuppyBeat"
  Obituary "%o was beat down by an Ettin."
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    CETN AA 5 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    CETN ABCD 3 A_Chase
    Loop
  Pain:
    CETN H 7 A_Pain
    Goto See
  Melee:
    CETN EF 3 A_FaceTarget
    CETN G 4 A_CustomMeleeAttack(random(1,8)*4, "EttinHit")
    Goto See
  Missile: //this tends to miss flying targets, so use this attack at your discretion!  Added "OFFSETPITCH" to compensate somewhat.
	CETN EF 3 A_FaceTarget
	CETN G 4 A_CustomMissile(EttinMaceProjectile, 40, 0, 0, CMF_OFFSETPITCH, 10)
	Goto See
  Death:
    CETN IJ 4
    CETN K 4 A_Scream
    CETN L 4 A_NoBlocking
    CETN M 4 A_QueueCorpse
    CETN NOP 4
    CETN Q -1
    Stop
  XDeath:
    CETN R 4
    CETN S 4 A_NoBlocking
    CETN T 4 A_SpawnItemEx("EttinMace", 0, 0, 8.5, random[DropMace](-128, 127)*0.03125,
                           random[DropMace](-128, 127)*0.03125, 10+random[DropMace](0, 255)*0.015625, 0,
                           SXF_ABSOLUTEVELOCITY)
    CETN U 4 A_Scream
    CETN V 4 A_QueueCorpse
    CETN "WXYZ[" 4
    CETN "\" -1
    Stop
  Ice:
    CETN "]" 5 A_FreezeDeath
    CETN "]" 1 A_FreezeDeathChunks
    Wait
  }
}

			Stop

			ZFOD KJI 5
			Goto See
	}

			stop
	}
}

ACTOR Uberchain
{
	Health 150
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Speed 4
	PainChance 100
	Mass 400
	+FLOORCLIP
	+SEEINVISIBLE
	Monster
	SeeSound "UCHAIN/Sight"
	ActiveSound "UCHAIN/Idle"
	PainSound "UCHAIN/Pain"
	Obituary "%o was riddled with holes by the Uber Chaingunner."
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			UCHW AABB 6 A_Look
			loop
		See:
			UCHW AAABBBCCCDDD 4 A_Chase
			loop
		Missile:
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("UCHAIN/Windup")
			UCHF A 20 A_FaceTarget
			Goto Missile1
		Missile1:
			UCHF AA 1
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("UCHAIN/Loop")
			UCHF B 1 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("UberTracer",32,0, random(4, -4), CMF_OFFSETPITCH, random(2, -2))
			TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("Smoke",20,10,32,1,0,1,0,0,0,0)
			UCHF B 1 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("UberTracer",32,0, random(4, -4), CMF_OFFSETPITCH, random(2, -2))
			UCHF A 0 A_MonsterRefire(130,"CoolDown")
			Goto Missile1+1
		CoolDown:
			UCHF A 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("UCHAIN/Winddown")
			UCHF A 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("UCHAIN/Steam")
			UCHF AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_SpawnItemEx("Smoke",20,10,32,random(2,-2),random(2,-2),random(1,3),0,0,0,0)
			Goto See
		Pain:
			UCHH A 2 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Death:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(130, "OtherDeath")
			TNT1 A 0 A_Playsound("UCHAIN/Death")
			UCD1 A 6 A_NoBlocking
			UCD1 BCDEF 6
			UCD1 F -1
			Stop
		OtherDeath:
			TNT1 A 0 A_Playsound("UCHAIN/Death")
			UCD3 A 6 A_NoBlocking
			UCD3 BCDEFG 6
			UCD3 G -1
			Stop
		XDeath:
			TNT1 A 0 A_XScream
			UCD2 A 6 A_NoBlocking
			UCD2 BCDEF 6
			UCD2 F -1
			Stop
		Raise:
			UCD1 F 5
			UCD1 FEDCBA 6
			Goto See
	}
}

Actor UberTracer : FastProjectile
{
	Projectile
	speed 90
	damage (3)
	scale 0.75
	RenderStyle Add
	Alpha 0.5
	SeeSound "Weapon/Machinegunfire"
	
	+BLOODSPLATTER
	+THRUGHOST
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			PUFF A 1 BRIGHT A_Quake(3,4,0,100,0)
			Loop
		Death:
			PUFF B 0 A_SetScale(1.0)
			PUFF B 1 A_PlaySound("UCHAIN/Bullets")
			PUFF C 1
			PUFF D 1
			Stop
	}
}

Actor ImpWarlord // Simply Hard ActiveBox version
{
    Health 180
    Radius 20
    Height 56
    Speed 10
    PainChance 60
	MeleeThreshold 196
	scale 1.1
    Monster
    +FLOORCLIP
	+DONTRIP
	+THRUSPECIES
    SeeSound "imp/sight"
    PainSound "imp/pain"
    DeathSound "imp/death"
    ActiveSound "imp/active"
    Obituary "%o couldn't run from the imp warlord's fireball."
    HitObituary "%o was beaten to death by an imp warlord."
    States
    {
    Spawn:
        WARL AB 10 A_Look
        Loop
    See:
        WARL AABBCCDD 3 A_Chase
        Loop
    Melee:
        WARL E 6 A_FaceTarget
        TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("implord/maceswing")
        WARL F 4 A_FaceTarget
        WARL G 5 A_CustomMeleeAttack(Random(1,8)*7, "implord/macehit", "None")
        Goto See
    Pain:
        TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(128, 2)
        WARL H 8 A_Pain
        Goto See
	    WARL I 1
        TNT1 A 0 A_SetReflectiveInvulnerable
	    WARL IIIIII 4 A_FaceTarget
        TNT1 A 0 A_Jump(160, 5)
        WARL IIII 4 A_FaceTarget
        Goto Pain+4
        TNT1 A 0 A_UnSetReflectiveInvulnerable
	Goto See
    Death:
        TNT1 A 0 A_FaceTarget
        TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("WarlordMace", 0, 0, 32, 4, 0, 0, -90, 128)
        WARL R 8 A_SpawnItemEx("WarlordShield", 0, 0, 32, 5, 0, 0, 90, 128)
        WARL S 8 A_Scream
        WARL T 6
	    WARL U 6 A_Fall
        WARL V -1
        Stop
    Raise:
        WARL VU 8
        WARL TSR 6
        Goto See
    }
}

			ZKEL H 2 A_Recoil(-4)

			ZKEL I 6 A_SkelFist

	}

ACTOR Cryocubus
{
	Health 600
	Radius 48
	Height 64

	DeathSound "fatso/death"
	ActiveSound "fatso/active"
	Obituary "%o was frozen by the Cryocubus."
	var int user_isfiring;
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			HIEL AB 15 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			HIEL AABBCCDDEEFF 4 A_Chase
			Loop
		Melee:
			HIEL G 20  A_FatRaise
			HIEL G 0 A_Facetarget
			HIEL G 0 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,-24,0,3)
			HIEL H 2 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,24,0,3)
			HIEL G 0 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,-24,0,3)
			HIEL H 2 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,24,0,3)
			HIEL G 0 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,-24,0,3)
			HIEL H 2 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,24,0,3)
			HIEL G 0 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,-24,0,3)
			HIEL H 2 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,24,0,3)
			HIEL G 0 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,-24,0,3)
			HIEL H 2 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,24,0,3)
			HIEL G 0 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,-24,0,3)
			HIEL H 2 A_CustomMissile("LanzaHielo2",16,24,0,3)
			Goto See
		Missile:
			HIEL H 2 A_JumpIfCloser(300, "Melee")
			HIEL G 20 A_FatRaise
			HIEL G 5 A_Facetarget
			HIEL H 5 Bright A_FatAttack1("MancubusBall_Ice")
			HIEL HG 5
			HIEL H 10 Bright A_FatAttack2("MancubusBall_Ice")
			HIEL HG 5
			HIEL H 10 Bright A_FatAttack3("MancubusBall_Ice")
			HIEL HG 5
			Goto See
		Pain:
			HIEL J 3  A_SetUserVar("user_isfiring",0)
			HIEL J 3  A_Pain
			Goto See

			HIEL K 6
			HIEL L 6 A_Scream

			HIEL NOP 6
			HIEL P -1 A_BossDeath
			Stop
		Raise:
			HIEL R 5
			HIEL QPONMLK 5
			Goto See
	}
}

ACTOR Chainguncubus
{
	Health 600
	Radius 48
	Height 64
	Mass 1000
	Speed 8
	PainChance 80
	Monster
	+FLOORCLIP
	+BOSSDEATH
	DropItem "ClipBox"
	DropItem "Chaingun"
	SeeSound "fatso/sight"
	PainSound "fatso/pain"
	DeathSound "fatso/death"
	ActiveSound "fatso/active"
	Obituary "%o was shredded into ribbons by a Chainguncubus"
	States
	{
		Spawn:
			FOFO AB 15 A_Look
			Loop
		See:
			FOFO AABBCCDDEEFF 4 A_Chase
			Loop
		Missile:
			FOFO I 0 A_FatRaise
			FOFO I 20 A_PlaySound("UCHAIN/Windup", CHAN_AUTO)
			goto MissileLoop
		MissileLoop:
			FOFO G 1
			FOFO H 0 BRIGHT A_PlaySound("SSWFire", CHAN_WEAPON)
			FOFO H 0 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("UberTracer",32, 32, random(4, -4), CMF_OFFSETPITCH, random(2, -2))
			FOFO H 1 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("UberTracer",32, -32, random(4, -4), CMF_OFFSETPITCH, random(2, -2))
			FOFO I 1 A_SpawnItemEx("Smoke",20,10,32,1,0,1,0,0,0,0)
			FOFO G 0 BRIGHT A_PlaySound("SSWFire", CHAN_WEAPON)
			FOFO G 0 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("UberTracer",32, 32, random(4, -4), CMF_OFFSETPITCH, random(2, -2))
			FOFO G 1 BRIGHT A_CustomMissile("UberTracer",32, -32, random(4, -4), CMF_OFFSETPITCH, random(2, -2))
			FOFO A 0 A_MonsterRefire(130,"CoolDown")
			loop
		CoolDown:
			FOFO A 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("UCHAIN/Winddown", CHAN_AUTO)
			FOFO A 10
			TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("UCHAIN/Steam", CHAN_AUTO)
			FOFO AAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAAA 1 A_SpawnItemEx("Smoke",20,10,32,random(2,-2),random(2,-2),random(1,3),0,0,0,0)
			Goto See
		Pain:
			FOFO J 3
			FOFO J 3 A_Pain
			Goto See
		Death:
			FOFO K 6
			FOFO L 6 A_Scream
			FOFO M 6 A_NoBlocking
			FOFO NOPQRS 6
			FOFO T -1 A_BossDeath
			Stop
		Raise:
			FOFO R 5
			FOFO QPONMLK 5
			Goto See
	}
}
